Maybe I am the only one but this is one of the worst songs/medleys so far, simply because their voices have been modified too much. Sure, the 90s is all about synths and yes, Autotune was a thing too. But what I admired most by those five awesome singers was their ability to emulate many many of these effects simply with their voices and if they weren't able, they used to adapt and modify the song that it fits their abilities.  Here you can hear right from the start that all voices are heavily modified, effects used, sometimes that much that you can't recognize the real voice anymore.  As much as I like the 90s, as much as I like Pentatonix...they effed up here. You can do better...a lot better!
